msg:The location is lovely - ocean on one side and mountains on the other side. Landscaping is beautiful. Our villa was very private with the vegetation. Listening to the birds and seeing butterflies made the experience even better. Mia (reception) was available whenever we had questions/concerns. She was very professional and kind. Whenever we had food delivered, the delivery personnel was always efficient. Housekeeping was friendly and efficient. The spa was enjoyed by my daughter. She had a scrub and a water treatment which she loved. That's why the Banyan Tree is well-known for their lovely spa treatments. The personnel was great. However, they took away the foot treatment which was disappointing. Consider bringing it back. When checking out, Hickey's friendliness and humor ended our experience at the Banyan Tree on a nice note. I wish I had known the villa pool wasn't heated. Though the temperature was nice in December, it was too cold to swim in an unheated pool. The resort's main pool was available though. The outside tub didn't have working lights which prevented a better experience from happening. More care in the maintenance of the villa might be an idea. For example, our pool umbrella had rips in it and the patio pillows were stained. That's an easy fix. Breakfast was nice in the selection of food. I'm not quite sure how to describe the experience at the restaurant. It was assumed that we couldn't speak Chinese (a natural thought since we are foreigners). When my daughter (fluent Chinese-speaker) spoke Chinese, she was conversing nicely with one female server when all of a sudden another one tapped her on the arm to stop when she proceeded to speak to us in English. I'm not sure if she wanted to practice her English or thought my daughter's Chinese was bad. It was an odd experience. The most bizarre thing was when one of the cooks (Louis Gao) acted as a personal butler for a foreign guest. It was disturbing to the rest of us guests in how the foreigner was getting special treatment... even having salt and pepper put into separate dishes. (Salt and pepper shakers were on his table.) The chef was excluding the rest of the resort guests. Why was this foreign man favored? What made him so special? All of us, other foreign guests and Chinese guests, looked at the "show" with a feeling of disappointment. Please treat us all with the same courtesy.

Unbeatable location. And yet, despite the proximity to everything, its in a secluded bay and once you are inside the compound, you will bask in absolute tranquility.

We also appreciated the small details in the design - the height of the villa plants blocking anyone's sightline from seeing into the bathroom, the burbling brooks, the beach buffeted by an immaculately tended front lawn, the view from the pool into the lagoon with plants all around as if you're looking into your own private rainforest. Each detail seems well thought out and each view from this property is like a painting. 

Our biggest concern was the age of the property as has been pointed out in other reviews. While everything was certainly not immaculate, it wasn't drab either. The age almost gives it a certain lived-in, charming character. And they took good care of the property, with top notch service and warmth from every staff. Cherry took care of us and gave us many small delightful surprises during our stay. She handled every request we have promptly and was instrumental in making our stay truly unforgettable. Thank you so much, Cherry!

Improvement suggestion to put a proper clothes drying rack in the rooms. Now we got a normal rack on request and is was ok but should be standard in all rooms. Also the prices at the beach bar are excessive. Now we basically didnt buy anything since it was 58 rmb for a basic beer you pay 3 rmb for in the supermarket. Had it been 30-35 we probably would have bought a couple drinks every day so all in all its a loss for the property. Theres also a pack of geese roaming the property and they get kind of aggressive when you get close. We learned after a while that offense is the best way and they run away but could have been mentioned sice they are pretty big and intimidating birds at first :) Narrowminded people might find some issues in English communication at times but not a problem for us. Last but not least big thanks to the amazing staff, in particular Colin Rao who took great care of us throughout and also to Devin who helped out with a delivery. The entire breakfast staff is a benchmark for other hotels and they did truly a standup job but staff in general a notch up from the other luxury properties we went to here previously, so well done. Banyan Tree is definitely a top choice for our next stay in Sanya, thank you for a great experience!

msg:The most outstanding thing about Banyan Tree Sanya is the swimming pool. You can jump into the water as soon as you open the door. The water is clean and warm in this season. The biggest concern when staying in a hotel is that the air conditioner is cold. In this weather, the air conditioner is not turned on and the air conditioner is not working. One advantage of the Banyan Tree room is that the air conditioners in the bathroom and bedroom are separate. When sleeping, just turn on the air conditioner in the bathroom. It will not be cold. Hot, but not blown away.
Moreover, their service focuses on privacy. If you don't greet them, they will seem to not exist. If you need anything, you can contact them at any time, and your takeaway orders will be delivered to the door of your room. msg:I have always stayed at the Ritz-Carlton in Sanya before. This is my first trip to Sanya after the epidemic and I tried the Banyan Tree. I thought that the Banyan Tree has always been famous for its service, but the experience was really disappointing.
1. This is an all-villa hotel, but there is no butler service. I called in advance to verify the reservation information. I mentioned that it was my birthday and I had booked for four nights. I hoped to arrange a better room type, but I was told that it was impossible to arrange it during the peak season. Well, the row of sea-view villas in front of me cannot be arranged even if they are vacant. It is indeed the peak season.
2. When we arrived at the hotel, there was only one boy at the door, and there was no welcome ceremony because there were really no waiters. The girl at the front desk at check-in was lukewarm throughout the whole process, and she checked in like a robot. When I mentioned that I might have to check out a day earlier due to changes in my itinerary, she bluntly said that there was no refund, and that I would have to pay the full amount even if I didn't stay. Well, I can't understand it. I stayed in this hotel for three days and the occupancy rate may be less than 60%. It seems that refunds cannot be made because I have to make money.
3. The beach in the hotel is very poor. It is full of shells and pebbles. If you look closely, it is basically an artificial beach. There is a circle outside, otherwise it is just a rocky tidal flat, and it is impossible to go into the sea. Later, I couldn't bear it anymore and drove to the Ritz-Carlton, only to realize that the beach in Yalong Bay is the real beach.
4. The hotel facilities and equipment are obviously old, and the service staff just smile on the surface, which is not like the happy feeling of a resort hotel at all. There was no water in the swimming pool in the villa during this weather, it was too cold, and it was facing away from the sun and it was even colder. The fallen leaves in the swimming pool had not been collected for three days.
5. The breakfast was okay. The chef was more enthusiastic than the waiter, but after three days of eating, I really had no choice. After all, there were too few varieties.
6. Anyone can go on the plank road and swings in the sea included in the package. They are simply gimmicks.
7. Generally speaking, it is quite satisfactory, with privacy, poor beach, and rigid service. I do not recommend it and will not choose it again.

The beach in Banyan is the best place to enjoy the sunset in Sanya. The swing of net celebrities and the trestle reaching the center of the sea are particularly dazzling against the background of the sky full of colorful clouds.

As the earliest luxury brand hotel in Sanya, Banyan Tree has only 39 villas, which are hidden in 130,000 square meters of various tropical plants. Privacy is greatly guaranteed. The service is very attentive. The aunt who is responsible for hygiene said that the mineral water in the room is not enough to drink, and she immediately sent a lot of water. The water quality of the swimming pool in the room is excellent, and the housekeeper Nicole also thoughtfully sent a swimming ring. The turndown service features Banyan Tree's classic little turtles. The bathroom is large and has a double basin configuration, and there is a surfing pool in the backyard.

The breakfast at the hotel is very good. Although there are not too many varieties, the ingredients are of good quality. Serving time from 7:00 ‚Äì 11:00, see smoked salmon and more. Since the hotel is only full, there are only about 100 people, so the waiters in the restaurant can better serve the guests. The chef is of a high level, and will ask the guests if they have taboos and whether they are satisfied. The Hainanese special chee cheong fun and Zhapo vinegar are particularly authentic, but the taste is more delicious than the stalls in the market. It's arguably better than any hotel experience I've stayed in in Sanya.
  The public swimming pool of the hotel is also a wide circular swimming lane with a length of 260 meters. It walks through the tropical plant garden and the water quality is very clean. During the day, the roasting sun shines through the leaves, and the dappled light and shadow are projected onto the swimming pool. It will not feel boring to swim a few laps in this changing greenery.

It coincides with the hotel lawn BBQ on the weekend. The dishes are good and the taste is very good. The ice cream is delicious and the coconut can be supplied unlimitedly, and the price is not cheap. But the sunset afterglow as the background is also worth the price.
